  Labels    : Q2–Q4 2025 + Q1 2026 outperformance  (WRDS CRSP 2025)
  No external data sources — macro from FRED/hardcoded, returns from WRDS
  Forward-looking: Q[t] ratios → Q[t+1] outperformance (shift=-1)
  Reference: Ananthakumar & Sarkar (2017)

── METHODOLOGY NOTES ─────────────────────────────────────────────
  Data source       : 100% WRDS (Compustat + CRSP) — no external APIs
  Feature source    : WRDS Compustat 2025 (clean quarterly ratios)
  Delta features    : Q[t] – Q[t-1] for 10 key ratios (momentum signals)
  Label source      : WRDS CRSP 2025 — Outperform = (Q[t+1] return > SPY)
  Method            : VIF≤2.5 → PCA≥80% → Logistic Regression
  Winsorization     : 1st–99th percentile from training data only
  Market cap ths.   : Computed from training data only
  Cluster assignment: KMeans fitted on 2010–Q3 2024, applied to 2025
  Forward-looking   : Q[t] ratios → Q[t+1] outperformance (shift=-1)
